font-size:10pt;"><tr><td style="width:48px;"></td><td></td></tr><tr><td style="vertical-align:top"><div style="line-height:174%;font-size:12pt;padding-left:24px;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">&#8226;</font></div></td><td style="vertical-align:top;"><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">Raises 2015 Guidance </font></div></td></tr></table><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;padding-left:48px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;text-indent:48px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">ATLANTA, </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">July&#160;24, 2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;- Aaron's, Inc. (NYSE: AAN), a leader in the sales and lease ownership and specialty retailing of furniture, consumer electronics, home appliances and accessories, today announced revenues and earnings for the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">three and six</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;months ended </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">June&#160;30, 2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">.</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;text-indent:48px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">For the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">second quarter</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">, revenues </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">increased</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">16.1%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;to </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">$769.0 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;compared with </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">$662.5 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;for the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">second quarter</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">2014</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">. Net earnings </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">increased</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">to </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">$40.5 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;compared with </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">$8.5 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;in the prior year period. Diluted earnings per share were </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">$.56</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;compared with </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">$.12</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;for the same quarter last year. EBITDA for the Company was </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">$89.8 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;compared with </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">$43.0 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;a year ago.</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;text-indent:48px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">On a non-GAAP basis, net earnings for the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">second quarter</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">increased</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;to </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">$44.7 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;compared with </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">$27.2 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;for the same period in </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">2014</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">, and earnings per share assuming dilution </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">increased</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;to </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">$.61</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;compared with </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">$.37</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;a year ago. In </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">, non-GAAP net earnings and diluted earnings per share exclude the effects of amortization expense resulting from the acquisition of Progressive. In </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">2014</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">, in addition to Progressive amortization, non-GAAP results exclude the effects of certain one-time Progressive transaction costs, financial advisory and legal costs related to addressing strategic matters and restructuring charges related to store </font></div><br><div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:right;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">1</font></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><a name="s060A7CD8DAE42426C1CDFC82F3ACD219"></a><div></div><br><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">closures. See &#8220;Use of Non-GAAP Information&#8221; and the related non-GAAP reconciliation accompanying this press release. </font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;text-indent:48px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#8220;The second quarter demonstrated our organization&#8217;s ability to grow revenues and increase EBITDA at double-digit rates,&#8221; said John Robinson, Chief Executive Officer of Aaron&#8217;s, Inc. &#8220;Our core business achieved an increase in profit margin due to improved expense and inventory control. We're disappointed that core revenues were not stronger in the quarter but remain optimistic that recent initiatives will drive better year-over-year comps in the future.&#8221; </font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;text-indent:48px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#8220;Progressive delivered an outstanding quarter with strong revenues and improved operating margins,&#8221; continued Mr. Robinson.&#160;&#160;&#8220;Our pipeline of new retailers is robust, and we're beginning to reap real benefits from the integration of the two businesses.&#160;Overall, the opportunity to grow Progressive remains exciting, and we'll maintain discipline in our core business until revenue initiatives gain more traction,&#8221; Mr. Robinson said.</font></div><a name="s7C685225A5DCC608B529FC82F3EA3898"></a><div style="line-height:174%;padding-top:8px;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Financial Summary</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;text-indent:48px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">During the first </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">six months</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">, revenues increased </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">27.5%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;to </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">$1.591 billion</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;compared with </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">$1.248 billion</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;for the first </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">six months</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">2014</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">. The </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">decrease</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;in the Company's franchise royalties and fees are primarily the result of a </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">decrease</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;in revenues of the Company's franchisees. Franchisees had revenues of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">$237.1 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;during the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">second quarter</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;and </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">$497.9 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;for the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">six months</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">, decreases of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">2.3%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;and </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">3.1%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">, respectively, from the comparable </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">2014</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;periods. Same store revenues and customer counts for franchised stores were </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">down</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">1.6%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;and </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">2.2%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">, respectively, for the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">second quarter</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;compared with the same quarter last year (revenues and customers of franchisees, however, are not revenues and customers of Aaron's, Inc.). Non-retail sales, which are primarily sales of merchandise to Aaron's Sales and Lease Ownership franchisees, </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">increased</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">.7%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;for the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">second quarter</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;and </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">2.8%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;for the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">six months</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;compared with the same periods last year.</font></div><a name="sE3B01944022C3521E3F7FC82F4865929"></a><div style="line-height:174%;padding-top:8px;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Store Count</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;text-indent:48px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">During the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">second quarter</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">, the Company opened </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">four</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;Company-operated Aaron's Sales &amp; Lease Ownership stores and </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">three</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;franchised stores. The Company acquired </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">seven</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;Aaron's Sales &amp; Lease Ownership stores from franchisees and sold </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">four</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;Company-operated Aaron's Sales &amp; Lease Ownership stores to franchisees, one of which was merged with an existing franchised location. </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">Twenty-five</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;Company-operated Aaron's Sales &amp; Lease Ownership stores and </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">three</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;franchised Aaron's Sales &amp; Lease Ownership stores were closed during the quarter. The Company also completed a </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">six</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;store swap with a third party during the quarter and merged the acquired stores with existing locations.</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;text-indent:48px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">At </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">June&#160;30, 2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">, the Company had </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">1,211</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;Company-operated Aaron's Sales &amp; Lease Ownership stores, </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">784</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;franchised Aaron's Sales &amp; Lease Ownership stores, </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">83</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;Company-operated HomeSmart stores, and </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">two</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;franchised HomeSmart stores. The total number of stores open at </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">June&#160;30, 2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;was </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">2,080</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">.</font></div><a name="sB45E6E56A4B69583FAE4FC82F4A57E70"></a><div style="line-height:174%;padding-top:8px;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">2015 Outlook</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;text-indent:48px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">The Company is updating its EBITDA and diluted earnings per share guidance for the full year 2015. No change is being made to the revenue guidance previously published on April </font></div><br><div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:right;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">4</font></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div><br><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">24, 2015. The webcast will be archived for playback at that same site.</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;padding-top:8px;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">About&#160;Aaron's, Inc.</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;text-indent:48px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">Aaron's, Inc.&#160;(NYSE: AAN), a leader in the sales and lease ownership and specialty retailing of furniture, consumer electronics, home appliances and accessories, has more than 2,000 Company-operated and franchised stores in 48 states, the District of Columbia, and&#160;Canada.&#160;Aaron's&#160;was founded in 1955, is headquartered in&#160;Atlanta&#160;and has been publicly traded since 1982. Progressive Leasing, a wholly-owned subsidiary and leading virtual lease-to-own company, provides lease-purchase solutions through more than 16,000 retail locations in 46 states. Aaron's, Inc.&#160;includes the Aarons.com, ShopHomeSmart.com and ProgLeasing.com brands. For more information, visit&#160;www.aarons.com.&#160; </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;text-indent:48px;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><br><div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:right;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">5</font></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div><br><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;text-indent:48px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-style:italic;">&#32;&#8220;Safe Harbor&#8221; Statement under the Private Securities Litigation Reform Act of 1995: Statements in this news release regarding Aaron's, Inc.'s business that are not historical facts are &#8220;forward-looking statements&#8221; that involve risks and uncertainties which could cause actual results to differ materially from those contained in the forward-looking statements.
